class="mw-body-content" id="siteNotice"><!-- CentralNotice --></div>\n<div class="mw-indicators mw-body-content">\n</div>\n<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">List of International Space Station expeditions</h1>\n<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">\n<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>\n<div id="contentSub"></div>\n<div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">\n\t\t\t\t\tJump to:\t\t\t\t\t<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, \t\t\t\t\t<a href="#p-search">search</a>\n</div>\n<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p>This is a chronological <b>list of expeditions to the <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">International Space Station</a> (ISS)</b>. All permanent ISS crews are named <span class="nowrap">"Expedition <i>n</i>"</span>, where <i>n</i> is sequentially increased with each expedition. Resupply mission crews and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Space_tourist" title="Space tourist">space tourists</a> are excluded (see <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_human_spaceflights_to_the_ISS" title="List of human spaceflights to the ISS">List of human spaceflights to the ISS</a> for details). ISS commanders are listed in <i>italics</i>. "Duration" refers to the crew and does not always correspond to "Flight up" or "Flight down".</p>\n<p></p>\n<div class="toc" id="toc">\n<div class="toctitle">\n<h2>Contents</h2>\n</div>\n<ul>\n<li href="#Current_expedition"><span class="tocnumber">2</span> <span class="toctext">Current expedition</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-3"><a href="#Future_expeditions"><span class="toctext">References</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</div>\n<p></p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Completed_expeditions">Completed expeditions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span This duration will measure the length of their cumulative stay in space from Expedition 43 through Expedition 46.</span></li>\n<li id="cite_note-7"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-7">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">This duration will measure the length of Soyuz TMA-18M from start to finish.</span></li>\n<li id="cite_note-15"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-15">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Whitson remained onboard the ISS for three extra months.
